Verdana">在现代社会的今天，人们都注重时间，讲究效率。快节奏的工作、生活方式在各个领域均有所展现。我们广大象棋爱好者，非常希望欣赏到精彩紧凑的国手演绎的速胜佳局，掌握一些速胜诀窍，在实战中释放博弈的激情，体验速胜的快感</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">局》。速胜局，棋界约定俗成的含义是指</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">25</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">回合以内的对局，速胜局的特点可以概括为</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">:</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">短小精悍，速战速决，奇巧妙绝，石破天惊。它们着法精练，节奏轻快，内涵丰富，千姿百态，或出奇制胜，或弃子搏杀，或兑子取势，或巧设陷阱，或连珠妙杀，或兼而有之。解拆它们，可以从中领会象棋多种战术的运用以及各种基本杀法技巧，读来令人爱不释手，啧啧称奇，在拍案叫绝的同时，达到开阔思路，提高棋艺的目的。</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; Verdana">象棋大师超群绝伦的棋艺，时而似涓涓细流，委婉起伏</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">;</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">时而如急风暴雨，惊涛拍岸</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">;</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: xml:lang="EN-US">;</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">那疾如闪电般的攻杀更叫人击节赞叹</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">!</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">这些都是象棋大师在烈的竞技比赛中的智慧结晶，是象棋艺术宝库中呕心沥血的艺术珍品</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">为使广大象棋爱好者对速胜局的发展有个系统全面的了解，我们精心撷取了五十多年象棋比赛各重要赛事，具有代表性的五十盘经典佳局，其中既有历届全国冠军之间的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">“</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">”</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">对话，也有新晋大师的成名佳局，浓缩体现了象坛五十多年来速胜局的发展历程，对于不同历史时期速胜局布局的演变与创新，各位象棋特级大师、大师所用变例及创新变化的不同特点与效果，我们尽力做到一定程度的概括与展现。</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US"><br />\xa0\xa0\xa0\xa0\xa0 </span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">书山有路勤为径，棋海无涯苦作舟。象棋是一门学问，需要刻苦学习，比赛磨炼，名师指点，才能学有所成我们希望广大读者能从本专辑受到启发，领略欣赏这一盘盘精彩的速胜法后，有</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">“</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">茅塞顿开</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">”</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">之功效，或有</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">“</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">借它山之石攻玉</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">”</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">之活用，从中领悟审局度势，调兵遣将，构思妙局，出奇制胜的诀窍，从而快速提高棋艺，战胜对手。</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">“</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">兵无常势，水无常形</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">”</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: Verdana">在现代社会的今天，人们都注重时间，讲究效率。快节奏的工作、生活方式在各个领域均有所展现。我们广大象棋爱好者，非常希望欣赏到精彩紧凑的国手演绎的速胜佳局，掌握一些速胜诀窍，在实战中释放博弈的激情，体验速胜的快感</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">!<br />\xa0\xa0\xa0\xa0\xa0\xa0 </span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">有鉴于此认本期我刊再度与杨瑞忠先生合作，一制作出了大型国手对局题材专辑</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">——</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">《新中国五</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">+</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">年经典速胜</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">50</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">局》。速胜局，棋界约定俗成的含义是指</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">25</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">回合以内的对局，速胜局的特点可以概括为</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">:</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">短小精悍，速战速决，奇巧妙绝，石破天惊。它们着法精练，节奏轻快，内涵丰富，千姿百态，或出奇制胜，或弃子搏杀，或兑子取势，或巧设陷阱，或连珠妙杀，或兼而有之。解拆它们，可以从中领会象棋多种战术的运用以及各种基本杀法技巧，读来令人爱不释手，啧啧称奇，在拍案叫绝的同时，达到开阔思路，提高棋艺的目的。</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US"><br />\xa0\xa0\xa0\xa0\xa0\xa0 </span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">漫步弈林速胜局，仿佛沉浸在一曲雄浑美妙的交响乐中</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">;</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">象棋大师超群绝伦的棋艺，时而似涓涓细流，委婉起伏</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">;</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">时而如急风暴雨，惊涛拍岸</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">;</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">那和风细雨般的细腻缠绵让人回味无穷</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">;</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">那疾如闪电般的攻杀更叫人击节赞叹</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">!</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">这些都是象棋大师在烈的竞技比赛中的智慧结晶，是象棋艺术宝库中呕心沥血的艺术珍品</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">!<br />\xa0\xa0\xa0\xa0\xa0\xa0</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">\xa0\xa0\xa0\xa0\xa0</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">为使广大象棋爱好者对速胜局的发展有个系统全面的了解，我们精心撷取了五十多年象棋比赛各重要赛事，具有代表性的五十盘经典佳局，其中既有历届全国冠军之间的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">“</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">强强</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">”</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">对话，也有新晋大师的成名佳局，浓缩体现了象坛五十多年来速胜局的发展历程，对于不同历史时期速胜局布局的演变与创新，各位象棋特级大师、大师所用变例及创新变化的不同特点与效果，我们尽力做到一定程度的概括与展现。</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US"><br />\xa0\xa0\xa0\xa0\xa0 </span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">书山有路勤为径，棋海无涯苦作舟。象棋是一门学问，需要刻苦学习，比赛磨炼，名师指点，才能学有所成我们希望广大读者能从本专辑受到启发，领略欣赏这一盘盘精彩的速胜法后，有</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">“</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">茅塞顿开</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">”</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">之功效，或有</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">“</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">借它山之石攻玉</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">”</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">之活用，从中领悟审局度势，调兵遣将，构思妙局，出奇制胜的诀窍，从而快速提高棋艺，战胜对手。</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">“</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">兵无常势，水无常形</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">”</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">，方寸棋盘，变幻无穷。在这美好的精神食粮面前，现在让我们一起穿越时空，感受经典，怀着欣悦的心情，细细品味，慢慢享受。</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US"><?xml:namespace prefix = o ns = "urn:schemas-microsoft-com:office:office" Verdana">短小精悍，速战速决，奇巧妙绝，石破天惊。它们着法精练，节奏轻快，内涵丰富，千姿百态，或出奇制胜，或弃子搏杀，或兑子取势，或巧设陷阱，或连珠妙杀，或兼而有之。解拆它们，可以从中领会象棋多种战术的运用以及各种基本杀法技巧，读来令人爱不释手，啧啧称奇，在拍案叫绝的同时，达到开阔思路，提高棋艺的目的。</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; Verdana">那和风细雨般的细腻缠绵让人回味无穷</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">;</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">那疾如闪电般的攻杀更叫人击节赞叹</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">!</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">这些都是象棋大师在烈的竞技比赛中的智慧结晶，是象棋艺术宝库中呕心沥血的艺术珍品</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">!<br />\xa0\xa0\xa0\xa0\xa0\xa0</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">\xa0\xa0\xa0\xa0\xa0</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">为使广大象棋爱好者对速胜局的发展有个系统全面的了解，我们精心撷取了五十多年象棋比赛各重要赛事，具有代表性的五十盘经典佳局，其中既有历届全国冠军之间的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">“</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">强强</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">”</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">对话，也有新晋大师的成名佳局，浓缩体现了象坛五十多年来速胜局的发展历程，对于不同历史时期速胜局布局的演变与创新，各位象棋特级大师、大师所用变例及创新变化的不同特点与效果，我们尽力做到一定程度的概括与展现。</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US"><br />\xa0\xa0\xa0\xa0\xa0 </span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">书山有路勤为径，棋海无涯苦作舟。象棋是一门学问，需要刻苦学习，比赛磨炼，名师指点，才能学有所成我们希望广大读者能从本专辑受到启发，领略欣赏这一盘盘精彩的速胜法后，有</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">“</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">茅塞顿开</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">”</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">之功效，或有</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">“</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">借它山之石攻玉</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">”</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">之活用，从中领悟审局度势，调兵遣将，构思妙局，出奇制胜的诀窍，从而快速提高棋艺，战胜对手。</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">“</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">兵无常势，水无常形</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-fareast-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US">”</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana">，方寸棋盘，变幻无穷。在这美好的精神食粮面前，现在让我们一起穿越时空，感受经典，怀着欣悦的心情，细细品味，慢慢享受。</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: Verdana; class="clearit"></div></div>&#13;\n<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; WIDOWS: 2; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; BACKGROUND-COLOR: rgb(255,255,255); TEXT-INDENT: 0px" class="articalInfo" auto="" word-spacing:="" 'time': '', 'author': '选自<棋艺> “ 楚河决生死，汉界争短长。斗智兼斗勇，胜负自明彰。 ” 棋场如战场，讲究兵贵神速。纹抨对坐，双方绞尽脑汁，想方设法，用最快的速度，最凌厉的杀招置对手于死地就象棋而言，下棋感到最愉悦最享受的地方，应该是入局绝杀的美妙时刻。 在现代社会的今天，人们都注重时间，讲究效率。快节奏的工作、生活方式在各个领域均有所展现。我们广大象棋爱好者，非常希望欣赏到精彩紧凑的国手演绎的速胜佳局，掌握一些速胜诀窍，在实战中释放博弈的激情，体验速胜的快感 ! 有鉴于此认本期我刊再度与杨瑞忠先生合作，一制作出了大型国手对局题材专辑 —— 《新中国五 + 年经典速胜 50 局》。速胜局，棋界约定俗成的含义是指 25 回合以内的对局，速胜局的特点可以概括为 : 短小精悍，速战速决，奇巧妙绝，石破天惊。它们着法精练，节奏轻快，内涵丰富，千姿百态，或出奇制胜，或弃子搏杀，或兑子取势，或巧设陷阱，或连珠妙杀，或兼而有之。解拆它们，可以从中领会象棋多种战术的运用以及各种基本杀法技巧，读来令人爱不释手，啧啧称奇，在拍案叫绝的同时，达到开阔思路，提高棋艺的目的。 漫步弈林速胜局，仿佛沉浸在一曲雄浑美妙的交响乐中 ; 象棋大师超群绝伦的棋艺，时而似涓涓细流，委婉起伏 ; 时而如急风暴雨，惊涛拍岸 ; 那和风细雨般的细腻缠绵让人回味无穷 ; 那疾如闪电般的攻杀更叫人击节赞叹 ! 这些都是象棋大师在烈的竞技比赛中的智慧结晶，是象棋艺术宝库中呕心沥血的艺术珍品 ! 为使广大象棋爱好者对速胜局的发展有个系统全面的了解，我们精心撷取了五十多年象棋比赛各重要赛事，具有代表性的五十盘经典佳局，其中既有历届全国冠军之间的 “ 强强 ” 对话，也有新晋大师的成名佳局，浓缩体现了象坛五十多年来速胜局的发展历程，对于不同历史时期速胜局布局的演变与创新，各位象棋特级大师、大师所用变例及创新变化的不同特点与效果，我们尽力做到一定程度的概括与展现。 书山有路勤为径，棋海无涯苦作舟。象棋是一门学问，需要刻苦学习，比赛磨炼，名师指点，才能学有所成我们希望广大读者能从本专辑受到启发，领略欣赏这一盘盘精彩的速胜法后，有 “ 茅塞顿开 ” 之功效，或有 “ 借它山之石攻玉 ” 之活用，从中领悟审局度势，调兵遣将，构思妙局，出奇制胜的诀窍，从而快速提高棋艺，战胜对手。 “ 兵无常势，水无常形 ” ，方寸棋盘，变幻无穷。在这美好的精神食粮面前，现在让我们一起穿越时空，感受经典，怀着欣悦的心情，细细品味，慢慢享受。 prefix = o ns = "urn:schemas-microsoft-com:office:office" /
